        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer539085667" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10954624716638791495">I wish I could of written this when I finished the book in the wee morning hours, when my heart was racing & I was feeling all kinds of emotions. I have calmed down since then. Let me start by saying I’m pretty sure I am turning a new leaf by going into books blind, I feel like the less I know the better the experience. If I already know if there is a HEA then how can I appreciate all the feelings that come with it? When We Collide was everything I was looking for & going in blind only made the </span>
  <span id="freeText10954624716638791495" style="display:none">I wish I could of written this when I finished the book in the wee morning hours, when my heart was racing &amp; I was feeling all kinds of emotions. I have calmed down since then. Let me start by saying I’m pretty sure I am turning a new leaf by going into books blind, I feel like the less I know the better the experience. If I already know if there is a HEA then how can I appreciate all the feelings that come with it? When We Collide was everything I was looking for &amp; going in blind only made the experience so worth it. I would not say this is a “dark read” (and I love those) but if you are looking for rainbows &amp; butterflies this book is not for you. It deals with difficult issues &amp; the author writes so amazingly, you feel everything. I already said previously I felt like I could see, taste &amp; touch. The book goes from past to present &amp; from his POV to hers and never once did I feel confused or mixed up. The flow was perfect! This is my first A.L Jackson book &amp; I will definitely be reading more from this very talented author. My heart was racing; I was nervous, happy, sad. Hell I just freaking loved it! I don’t know if it’s just a case of the right book at the right time for me, however…. Finally a book I can add to my 5 star shelf. Ohhh and best of all ladies it’s a stand-alone.</span>

<div id="review_465447290" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">

              <span id="reviewTextContainer465447290" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer10713708319764707521">I was so into this book in the beginning , then somewhere in the middle I started to get bored with it .. but I stuck with it and BOY am I glad I did WHAT AN AMAZINGLY AWESOME READ !!!!<br/><br/><b>“I don’t know how to stop loving you.”</b><br/><br/>William has spent six years running from his past and the last eight months trying to rid his mind of the dreams that increasingly haunt his nights. Trapped in a world of false ambitions and feigned affections, William knows he’s reached a breaking point and something’s going </span>
  <span id="freeText10713708319764707521" style="display:none">I was so into this book in the beginning , then somewhere in the middle I started to get bored with it .. but I stuck with it and BOY am I glad I did WHAT AN AMAZINGLY AWESOME READ !!!!<br /><br /><b>“I don’t know how to stop loving you.”</b><br /><br />William has spent six years running from his past and the last eight months trying to rid his mind of the dreams that increasingly haunt his nights. Trapped in a world of false ambitions and feigned affections, William knows he’s reached a breaking point and something’s going to give.<br /><br />Maggie had lived her entire life without hope until one man showed her what it meant to be loved. He’d been her light in a lifetime of darkness. Six years ago, that darkness stole him away. Without him, she’s surrendered herself to an existence she doesn’t know how to escape.<br /><br />When the family William left behind is struck by tragedy, he is called back to the one place he’s sworn to never return to again. <br /><br />In a moment that will change his life forever, William comes face to face with the girl who, with one look, captured his heart. He is unable to ignore the buried desires and the hope for the future they’d once believed they’d have. <br /><br />Now William is ready to fight to take back what had been stolen from him six years before.<br />But he never imagined what that fight might cost him. <br /><br /><br /><b>“I loved her. Oh God… I loved her. She was everything, ripped me apart and made me whole.”</b> <br /><br />I really loved this story. It's definitely an Emotional one, but it's one that I'm glad to have read as there is Love, the kind that seeps through the pages and just grabs at you, the kind that just makes you feel good, so this is one Worth Reading!<br /><br /> Now,the characters were so well written. Maggie , She's shy, kind, but is in a relationship that's just so abusive at times, it was just shocking at what this guy had done to her, and in ways I found her story just really believable as she's basically with someone that is just like her Father and I think I really saw Maggie grow to be a stronger character, you'll read what move she finally makes.<br /><br />From the beginning I knew things were going to be rough for William. The turmoil that raged within him was too much to be held inside, and at some point he was bound to snap. But the way he reacted to his circumstances was real and believable. I immediately wanted to know more about his past and how he came to be the person he was. Will was a very layered character, and I gravitated towards him without hesitation. Maybe it was his flaws. Or maybe it was the fact that he knew he needed to change some things about himself that made his character all the more appealing. Either way, I loved his point of view and his development throughout the story.<br /><br /><b>“Because it shouldn't hurt to be touched.” </b><br /><br />Troy is a demeaning and abusive man, who takes what he wants when he wants it not caring who he hurts in his path of destruction. He truly was the bad seed in this book .. It would of been nice to have a little of his past to see what led him to be the way that he was ...<br /><br /><br />Great Read for sure My Favorite one of A.L. Jackson's for sure <br /><br /><br /><br /><br /></span>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Janna ♥ I&#39;m A Sweet And Sassy Book Whore ♥" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Janna ♥ I&#39;m A Sweet And Sassy Book Whore ♥" href="/user/show/6903437-janna-i-m-a-sweet-and-sassy-book-whore">Janna ♥ I&#39;m A Sweet And Sassy Book Whore ♥</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9781938404276" href="/book/show/15826457-when-we-collide">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer393634100" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17963517815666095098"><br/> <br/> This review will also be posted at <a target='_blank' rel='noopener nofollow' href='http://www.mysecretromancebookreviews.com'>www.mysecretromancebookreviews.com</a><br/><br/>William left his family and his home town 6 years ago and never looked back at the reminder of what he lost and the pain he felt. He was broken inside and angry at the world and especially at Maggie. He lived in an unhappy life and had a job he hated… he was living one miserable day at a time. The dreams that wake him every night are haunting him and do not make any sense, or are they not dreams but something else? William fi</span>
  <span id="freeText17963517815666095098" style="display:none"><br /> <br /> This review will also be posted at <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.mysecretromancebookreviews.com">www.mysecretromancebookreviews.com</a><br /><br />William left his family and his home town 6 years ago and never looked back at the reminder of what he lost and the pain he felt. He was broken inside and angry at the world and especially at Maggie. He lived in an unhappy life and had a job he hated… he was living one miserable day at a time. The dreams that wake him every night are haunting him and do not make any sense, or are they not dreams but something else? William finally came back home for a short visit, but stayed longer than planned because a chance encounter has now changed everything he once believed. While his family loves him, they don’t know what happened all those years ago and worry that he will leave again and not look back. He has a hard fight ahead of him and a dangerous one as well, but he doesn’t care he only wants the wrongs of the past to be righted.<br /><br />Maggie, oh Maggie the life you were forced to live is one I would never wish on another living being. You did what you had to do to protect the ones you loved and sacrificed your own peace, happiness and worth to do it. My heart broke for Maggie so many times that I couldn’t help but feel the pain of the abused she was forced to live through. She is so broken and fragile but at the same time so very strong to do whatever it takes to protect the most precious person in her life, her son, even from the devil himself…. A mother’s love is something so powerful that words cannot begin to describe it.<br /><br />When Maggie and William still feel the connection and bond that is there between them, even from a distance, they know that the only way to find happiness and the love that they have been missing is to find a way to be together so that they can begin to heal the new and old pains. Will William’s love be able to heal Maggie from all that she has been through or is she too far broken and beaten? There is an old saying that goes “love heals all wounds”, and I have always believed that to be true. A.L. Jackson has proven once again that love does indeed heal all wounds, both physical and emotional when the love that is given is pure and true. Books like Pulled, Take This Regret, and now, When We Collide pull at our emotions and hearts, they show us that love isn’t always perfect and mistake free, and love can hurt on many different levels, but true love is worth the fight we face to finally be happy in the end.<br /></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer9462323970479841594">A.L. Jackson has done it again. When We Collide is PHENOMINAL!!!!! I don't know how she does it but every book I have read by her has pulled at every hearts string I have. This one was even harder for me because of the sensitivity of the subject matter. I have to say she made me feel everything Maggie and William felt throughout the entire book. I felt like I was a part of the story. I have to say Troy was a real douchebag.   <span id="freeText9462323970479841594" style="display:none">A.L. Jackson has done it again. When We Collide is PHENOMINAL!!!!! I don't know how she does it but every book I have read by her has pulled at every hearts string I have. This one was even harder for me because of the sensitivity of the subject matter. I have to say she made me feel everything Maggie and William felt throughout the entire book. I felt like I was a part of the story. I have to say Troy was a real douchebag. I don't feel bad for him at all for what happens to him in the book. I truly felt Maggie's pain and suffering, I felt so bad for her. She wanted to make things better but Troy just kept pushing all the right buttons to manipulate her to what he wanted. I do wish that William would have stuck with his instincts a little more, probably could have avoiding some of the things that happened. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ I know I can't blame him and I don't really but I don't understand how he can say he knew she was lying but then still run away. I know in the end he feels bad about it but I still wish he would have fought harder for her.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br />I would definitely recommend this book to anyone who loved Pulled and Take This Regret.<br /><br />This will for sure have a spot on my favs shelf:)</span>

Are the odds against them? Are their issues insurmountable? The book is filled with much anticipation and suspense. The supporting characters are wonderful too. <div id="review_1035601915" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1035601915" />
    <a title="Cassia Brightmore" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/30120017-cassia-brightmore"><img alt="Cassia Brightmore" src="https://s.gr-assets.com/assets/nophoto/user/f_50x66-6a03a5c12233c941481992b82eea8d23.png" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1035601915?book_show_action=true">Aug 24, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Cassia Brightmore" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Cassia Brightmore" href="/user/show/30120017-cassia-brightmore">Cassia Brightmore</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9781938404276" href="/book/show/15826457-when-we-collide">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/30120017-cassia-brightmore?shelf=arcs">arcs</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/30120017-cassia-brightmore?shelf=loved">loved</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1035601915" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16025563539480235330">There are books that you enjoy, and then there are books that <b>breathe life into you.</b> This is a story that touches the soul, that anchors you to the earth in bone-crushing sadness and sends you soaring through the clouds on the waves of true love. All through reading this book, my emotions tumbled over one another. I felt the angst, I experienced the anguish, I cowered in fear and I yelled in anger. When We Collide touches on those real raw moments in life that we all go through. Regret, shame, a</span>
  <span id="freeText16025563539480235330" style="display:none">There are books that you enjoy, and then there are books that <b>breathe life into you.</b> This is a story that touches the soul, that anchors you to the earth in bone-crushing sadness and sends you soaring through the clouds on the waves of true love. All through reading this book, my emotions tumbled over one another. I felt the angst, I experienced the anguish, I cowered in fear and I yelled in anger. When We Collide touches on those real raw moments in life that we all go through. Regret, shame, and impossible, gut-wrenching love. I couldn’t put this book down, I connected with the characters on so many levels. The storyline was built with pieces of originality, with plot twists and unforgettable moments that stole little pieces of my heart.<br /><br /><blockquote>
  <i>My heart had come alive and then been crushed in what had felt like the same breath.</i>
</blockquote><br /><br />William Marsch is a broken man. From the outside, he’s known as a man who has it all. A coveted top position with an LA firm, a beautiful, successful girlfriend - the world at his fingertips. And not one part of it mattered to him. He’s a man going through the motions, <b>burying his misery and the pain of regret.</b> Having his heart torn out years earlier has hardened him - forced him to turn his back on his family and shut them out of his life for 6 long years. As hard as he fights to forget, to burn the memory of her touch from his skin, she is always there. Her face taunts him from behind closed eyes, the sound of her voice torments his dreams, along with an unfamiliar child, fighting for his life. Maggie...the girl of his dreams, the girl that he fell helplessly in love with. And the girl that ultimately destroyed him.<br /><br /><blockquote>
  <i>I loved her. She was everything, ripped me apart and made me whole.</i>
</blockquote><br /><br />Maggie Krieger’s life has not been easy. At the mercy of her abusive father, she learned from a young age that the only way to avoid pain, was to hide - to be invisible. In a small town, that isn’t the easiest thing to do, the rumors of her horrific home life trailing behind her as a sinister reminder that she will never be good enough, that this is the life she is destined to lead. A fateful night has her path colliding with William’s - a handsome older boy who seemed to see right past her walls, his eyes telling her that she couldn’t hide from him. William’s interest in her is evident, and before long, Maggie begins to open parts of herself up, to let her real self shine through. Their path isn’t a simple one, <b>their growing love is tumultuous, their stolen moments forbidden.</b> When Maggie chooses to stay in the life she was handed, and not pursue a future with William, both of their worlds are irrevocably shattered – setting in motion a turnstile of events that will forever change their lives.<br /><br /><blockquote>
  <i>I’d fallen for the first time in my life and I’d fallen hard. That fall had left me battered and scarred.</i>
</blockquote><br /><br />This book was so emotional to me, when William returns to his home town years later and faces the life he lost, it brought me to tears. Just the pure anguish he felt, A.L. Jackson did a phenomenal job of portraying his sense of loss and regret. I loved the connection between William and Maggie, <b>their story spanned years</b> and when they finally come face to face, its as if no time has passed. Maggie is harboring a shocking secret however, and it has eerie similarity to the dreams that haunt William each night – a young boy. A six year old boy.<br /><br /><blockquote>
  <i>We collided, body and soul, mouths and hands and whispered pleas.</i>
</blockquote><br /><br />When the past and present collide once again – will the outcome be different? Can Maggie be saved from the life she wrongly chose all those years before? Who is this child that haunts Will’s subconscious at night? If you are looking for a read that will open your soul and leave you feeling raw and a little broken, this is a book for you. When We Collide is <b>a tale that heals as much as it hurts</b> and takes you on a journey with two very unforgettable characters. Experience this love story, its not one you will soon forget.<br /><br /><blockquote>
  <i>“You can’t leave before you get the chance to start.”</i>
</blockquote><br /><br />xo Cassia<br /><a href="http://deliciouslywickedbooks.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Deliciously Wicked Books</a><br /><a href="https://www.facebook.com/pages/Deliciously-Wicked-Books/844281025599841" rel="nofollow noopener">Find Me On Facebook</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="16025563539480235330" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer10168861313669065438"><b> "I'd lost myself somewhere along the way, and maybe my subconscious was telling me it was time I found that person again, because I was sure as hell wasn't happy with who I'd become." </b><br/><br/>I have been emotionally moved by many books. I have cried, I have been inconsolable, and my heart has hurt so much that I thought it might burst in my chest. However only A L Jackson has the power to make my heart hurt the whole time I am reading her story. Only she can write a story so moving that I basically can</span>
  <span id="freeText10168861313669065438" style="display:none"><b> "I'd lost myself somewhere along the way, and maybe my subconscious was telling me it was time I found that person again, because I was sure as hell wasn't happy with who I'd become." </b><br /><br />I have been emotionally moved by many books. I have cried, I have been inconsolable, and my heart has hurt so much that I thought it might burst in my chest. However only A L Jackson has the power to make my heart hurt the whole time I am reading her story. Only she can write a story so moving that I basically can't stop crying the whole way through. I knew what I was getting into when I picked this book up, I'd read the reviews and I also knew from experience in reading Take this Regret by Jackson that I was in for a massive tear-jerker, but this book took that whole idea to a new level. <br /><br />William and Maggie are both so broken. Maggie from a harsh life that no individual should have to experience and William from the scars left from getting his heart broken by Maggie six years ago. While many people have commented that they believed that the flicking between the past and the present was annoying and off putting for me it only added to the story. I liked not knowing all the details at once and I liked that Jackson gave enough time for us to fully see ever facade of Maggie and William turmulous relationship. <br /><br /><b> "Funny how the lies bled so easily from my mouth but the truth fought to remain hidden. But the lies had been ingrained so deeply through fear and shame they'd almost become my truth." </b><br /><br />In the beginning I wanted to scream at Maggie 'why?" and scream at William 'why?'. I couldn't understand how Maggie could just walk away, that wasn't unlill A L Jackson showed us exactly how everything occurred. We got to fully get to know both of these characters on every level to the point that we could understand their decisions while still being heartbroken from the regret both of them had at letting it all fall apart six years ago. <br /><br />Jackson takes the contemporary romance to a whole new level. A level where we are not just exploring a growing connection between two people, but where the reader is taken right into the emotional needs and physche of each character. She uses the changing point of view, and changing periods in time to take us on the emotional journey between two people and the decisions that people can make based on their own insecurities and broken history. She is a bloody genius and although I need to mentally prepare myself for her novels this is the exact thing that makes her amazing. In a world filled with cliche and stories that often leave me feeling cold, this book left me emotionally drained and satiated, and most of all, alive. <br /><br />Thank god for HEA!!<br /><br /><b> "It didn't mean our lives weren't filled with hardships, that each day there wasn't a small struggle we had to overcome or a giant obstacle we had to face. It just meant it was worth it." </b><br /><br /><br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="10168861313669065438" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/593739167?book_show_action=true">Apr 18, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/17412457-when-we-collide">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3715473-ann?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3715473-ann?shelf=romance-drama">romance-drama</a>
          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer593739167" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16822165374675886493">A story about William/Maggie’s lost love that comes full circle. It’s sad, dark, angsty and emotional with some big time drama. A heartache filled story that’s centered on Maggie’s life of domestic violence either at the hands of her father or her boyfriend-husband/Troy. There’s a child involved and that always gets to me. Tough one to get through. While William/Maggie finally get their HEA it’s a gut wrenching journey. In the end you’re left with realistic good feelings knowing this couple is o</span>
  <span id="freeText16822165374675886493" style="display:none">A story about William/Maggie’s lost love that comes full circle. It’s sad, dark, angsty and emotional with some big time drama. A heartache filled story that’s centered on Maggie’s life of domestic violence either at the hands of her father or her boyfriend-husband/Troy. There’s a child involved and that always gets to me. Tough one to get through. While William/Maggie finally get their HEA it’s a gut wrenching journey. In the end you’re left with realistic good feelings knowing this couple is on the mend with the love they both deserve. You also realize William, Maggie and little Jonathan have a long road ahead of them with all the mental/emotional/physical pain they’ve endured but that healing will surely come. While I’m a big fan of A. L. Jackson’s Take this Regret, When We Collide is not a bk I’ll want to put on my re-read list. Once down this road was enough for me. Feeling all over the place with this one, but I’m giving it 4 stars for a well written story. </span>
  <a data-text-id="16822165374675886493" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('NBpZ+a7wL08OEIhtc1wPL1ZhIQgKQSN3GCzNbGPt4gcqJWYJOqxSBzCMMoqENFt2NXKmz1YeH650taVeM/hhbg==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('EZC8EDfAWV53c58xC5DrgCAeo7GJeJI3O+NOXNkZJ7gPr4Pgo5wkFknvJdb8+L/ZQw0kdtUnru5XeiZuiQyk0Q==')})
  }

  <span id="freeText3793381787475315810" style="display:none">A.L. Jackson is the New York Times &amp; USA Today Bestselling author of contemporary romance.
